import datetime
from datetime import timedelta

df['event_time'] = pd.to_datetime(df['event_time'])
    
def conc_rate(data):
    suspect = []
    date_before = 0
    for date in data['event_time']:
        if(date_before == 0):
            data_check = data.loc[(data['event_time'] >= date) & (data['event_time'] <= date + timedelta(hours=1))]
            conc_rate = (len(data_check)) / (data_check['userid'].unique().size)
            
            if(conc_rate >= 3):
                mode = data_check['userid'].value_counts().iloc[0]

                for userid in data_check['userid'].unique():
                    if(data_check['userid'].value_counts()[userid] == mode):
                        if str(userid) not in suspect:
                            suspect.append(str(userid))
                        
        else:
            data_check = data.loc[(data['event_time'] >= date) & (data['event_time'] <= date + timedelta(hours=1))]
            date3 = copy.deepcopy(date)
            while(date3 > date_before):
                data_check = data.loc[(data['event_time'] >= date3) & (data['event_time'] <= date3 + timedelta(hours=1))]
                if(data_check['userid'].unique().size == 0):
                    break
                if((len(data_check)) / (data_check['userid'].unique().size) >= 3):
                    mode = data_check['userid'].value_counts().iloc[0]
            
                    for userid in data_check['userid'].unique():
                        if(data_check['userid'].value_counts()[userid] == mode):
                            if str(userid) not in suspect:
                                suspect.append(str(userid))
            
                flag = -2
                while((len(data_check)+flag >= 0) and (data_check.iloc[-1]['event_time'] == data_check.iloc[-2]['event_time'])):
                    flag = flag - 1
                    
                if(len(data_check)+flag < 0):
                    break
                
                delta = data_check.iloc[-1]['event_time'] - data_check.iloc[flag]['event_time']
                date3 = date3 - delta
                        
        date_before = copy.deepcopy(date)
    
    out_str = "&".join(suspect)
    return out_str

results = []
flagg = 1
for shop in unique_shops:
    print(flagg, ' ' , shop)
    flagg = flagg + 1
    shop_data = df.loc[df['shopid']==shop].sort_values('event_time', ascending=True)
    stri = conc_rate(shop_data)
    if(stri == ""):
        stri = "0"
    results.append(stri)
